\_sh v3.0  1082 Text

\id Grigoreva_NI_shkola_remesel_1_000_metadata
\ref Recorded on 28 June 2009 in Esso by Brigitte Pakendorf and Natalia Aralova. This was a very long recording session, which was
really only cut short due to our running out of video tape. The recording was done in the so-called 'crafts school', actually just a big
workshop in the house of Marina Voronova, a wood artist in Esso, who had for a few years directed a crafts school with the support
of some international grants. During the recording, Marina Voronova left the house to work in an outdoors studio; only NIG, BP
and NA were present in the workshop. NIG dressed up in her stage costume, and proceeded to give a one-man performance
including singing, which she accompanied on her traditional Ewen shaman's drum. NIG had prepared for the recording (it was
agreed upon nearly a week in advance), making a list of topics she wanted to cover. She didn't manage to cover everything she'd
planned to, however, since she digressed quite a bit. 
\qu ?????Transcribed and translated by ..... NIG????, Transcription and translation corrected by BP and Rimma Maksimovna Egorova in 2016,
glossed by BP in 2016. Funding by the Volkswagen Foundation (DoBeS grant) and CNRS/UniversitÈ Lyon 2 (laboratoire DDL). Speaker
abbreviation = NIG
\ref Natalja Ionovna Grigor'eva (Ichanga) was born in 1956, i.e. she was 53-54 at the time of the recording. She had first trained as a
leather worker, but later gone on to get a higher education as an actor and director of spectacles. She speaks Russian with her
husband and children.

about it...), Rimma said it should be "meÀêndeƒçiƒç" and that there is no word "meÀêndeƒç", only "meÀêndeƒçiƒç" - so I ended up entering that as a separate lexeme (I just don't think it's so important to
